create fine if not present\n        existing_fine = next((f for f in fines if f['borrow_id'] == borrow_id and f['username'] == current_user and f['status'] == 'Unpaid'), None)\n        if not existing_fine and borrow['fine_amount'] > 0:\n            # Create new fine\n            new_fine_id = max([f['fine_id'] for f in fines], default=0) + 1\n            fine_record = {\n                'fine_id': new_fine_id,\n                'username': current_user,\n                'borrow_id': borrow_id,\n                'amount': borrow['fine_amount'],\n                'status': 'Unpaid',\n                'date_issued': date_to_str(datetime.now().date())\n            }\n            fines.append(fine_record)\n            write_fines(fines)\n        # Status remains Overdue (not full returned because of fine unpaid)\n    else:\n        borrow['status'] = 'Returned'\n\n    write_borrowings(borrowings)\n\n    # Update book status to Available\n    for b in books:\n        if b['book_id'] == borrow['book_id']:\n            b['status'] = 'Available'\n            break\n    write_books(books)\n\n    borrow_context = {\n        'borrow_id': borrow['borrow_id'],\n        'book_id': borrow['book_id'],\n        'title': next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == borrow['book_id']), 'Unknown'),\n        'return_date': borrow['return_date'],\n        'status': borrow['status'],\n        'fine_amount': borrow['fine_amount']\n    }\n\n    flash('Book return processed. Thank you!')\n    return render_template('return_confirmation.html', borrow=borrow_context)\n\n# 9. my_reservations_page - GET /my_reservations\n@app.route('/my_reservations')\ndef my_reservations_page():\n    reservations = read_reservations()\n    books = read_books()\n\n    user_reservs = [r for r in reservations if r['username'] == current_user]\n\n    reservation_context = []\n    for r in user_reservs:\n        book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), None)\n        title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'\n        reservation_context.append({\n            'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],\n            'book_id': r['book_id'],\n            'title': title,\n            'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],\n            'status': r['status']\n        })\n\n    return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=reservation_context)\n\n# 10. cancel_reservation - POST /cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>\n@app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])\ndef cancel_reservation(reservation_id):\n    reservations = read_reservations()\n    res = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id and r['username'] == current_user), None)\n    if not res:\n        flash('Reservation not found.')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reservations_page'))\n\n    if res['status'] == 'Cancelled':\n        flash('Reservation already cancelled.')\n        return redirect(url_for('my_reservations_page'))\n\n    res['status'] = 'Cancelled'\n    write_reservations(reservations)\n\n    flash('Reservation cancelled successfully.')\n\n    # After cancellation, reload updated reservations list\n    return my_reservations_page()\n\n# 11. my_reviews_page - GET /my_reviews\n@app.route('/my_reviews')\ndef my_reviews_page():\n    reviews = read_reviews()\n    books = read_books()\n\n    user_reviews = [r for r in reviews if r['username'] == current_user]\n    reviews_context = []\n    for r in user_reviews:\n        book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), None)\n        book_title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'\n        reviews_context.append({\n            'review_id': r['review_id'],\n            'book_title': book_title,\n            'rating': r['rating'],\n            'review_text': r['review_text']\n        })\n    return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=reviews_context)\n\n# 12 & 13. write_review_page(GET), submit_review(POST) for /write_review/<int:book_id>\n@app.route('/write_review/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef write_review_page(book_id):\n    books = read_books()\n    book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)\n    if not book:\n        flash('Book not found.')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))\n\n    # POST: process submitted review\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        rating_raw = request.form.get('rating')\n        review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()\n\n        try:\n            rating = int(rating_raw)\n            if rating < 1 or rating > 5:\n                flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.')\n                return render_template('write_review.html', book={ 'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']})\n        except:\n            flash('Invalid rating value.')\n            return render_template('write_review.html', book={ 'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']})\n\n        if not review_text:\n            flash('Review text cannot be empty.')\n            return render_template('write_review.html', book={ 'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']})\n\n        reviews = read_reviews()\n\n        # Check if user has already reviewed this book (exact specification does not clarify if editing or multiple allowed, assuming edit allowed)\n        existing_review = next((r for r in reviews if r['username'] == current_user and r['book_id'] == book_id), None)\n\n        today_str = datetime.now().date().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')\n\n        if existing_review:\n            # Update existing review\n            existing_review['rating'] = rating\n            existing_review['review_text'] = review_text\n            existing_review['review_date'] = today_str\n        else:\n            # Add new review\n            new_review_id = max([r['review_id'] for r in reviews], default=0) + 1\n            new_review = {\n                'review_id': new_review_id,\n                'username': current_user,\n                'book_id': book_id,\n                'rating': rating,\n                'review_text': review_text,\n                'review_date': today_str\n            }\n            reviews.append(new_review)\n\n        write_reviews(reviews)\n\n        flash('Your review has been submitted.')\n        return redirect(url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book_id))\n\n    # GET: display review form\n    simple_book = {\n        'book_id': book['book_id'],\n        'title': book['title'],\n        'author': book['author']\n    }\n    return render_template('write_review.html', book=simple_book)\n\n# 14. user_profile_page - GET /profile\n@app.route('/profile')\ndef user_profile_page():\n    users = read_users()\n    user_profile = next((u for u in users if u['username'] == current_user), None)\n    if not user_profile:\n        flash('User profile not found.')\n        return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))\n\n    borrowings = read_borrowings()\n    books = read_books()\n\n    user_borrow_history = [b for b in borrowings if b['username'] == current_user and b['status'] in ('Returned', 'Overdue')]\n    borrow_history_context = []\n    for b in user_borrow_history:\n        book = next((bk for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), None)\n        title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'\n        borrow_history_context.append({\n            'book_id': b['book_id'],\n            'title': title,\n            'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],\n            'return_date': b['return_date']\n        })\n\n    return render_template('profile.html', user_profile=user_profile, borrow_history=borrow_history_context)\n\n# 15. update_profile - POST /profile/update\n@app.route('/profile/update', methods=['POST'])\ndef update_profile():\n    email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()\n    phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()\n    address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()\n\n    users = read_users()\n    user_profile = next((u for u in users if u['username'] == current_user), None)\n\n    if not user_profile:\n        flash('User profile not found.')\n        return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))\n\n    # Validate basic email presence\n    if not email:\n        flash('Email cannot be empty.')\n        return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))\n\n    user_profile['email'] = email\n    user_profile['phone'] = phone\n    user_profile['address'] = address\n\n    write_users(users)\n\n    flash('Profile updated successfully.')\n    return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))\n\n# 16. payment_confirmation_page - GET /payment/<int:fine_id>\n@app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['GET'])\ndef payment_confirmation_page(fine_id):\n    fines = read_fines()\n    fine = next((f for f in fines if f['fine_id'] == fine_id and f['username'] == current_user), None)\n    if not fine:\n        flash('Fine record not found.')\n        return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))\n\n    fine_context = {\n        'fine_id': fine['fine_id'],\n        'amount': fine['amount']\n    }\n\n    return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine=fine_context)\n\n# 17. confirm_payment - POST /payment/<int:fine_id>\n@app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['POST'])\ndef confirm_payment(fine_id):\n    fines = read_fines()\n    borrowings = read_borrowings()\n\n    fine = next((f for f in fines if f['fine_id'] == fine_id and f['username'] == current_user), None)\n    if not fine:\n        flash('Fine record not found.')\n        return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))\n\n    if fine['status'] == 'Paid':\n        flash('This fine has already been paid.')\n        return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))\n\n    # Mark fine as paid\n    fine['status'] = 'Paid'\n\n    # Also update borrowings status: if overdue and paid, mark as Returned\n    borrow = next((b for b in borrowings if b['borrow_id'] == fine['borrow_id']), None)\n    if borrow and borrow['status'] == 'Overdue':\n        borrow['status'] = 'Returned'\n\n    write_fines(fines)\n    write_borrowings(borrowings)\n\n    flash('Fine payment successful. Thank you!')\n    return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app.run(debug=True)\n",

         === app.py ===
         from flask import Flask, render_template, request, redirect, url_for, flash, session
         from datetime import datetime, timedelta
         import os
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'your_secret_key'
         
         data_dir = 'data'
         
         # Helper functions to convert date formats
         
         def str_to_date(dstr):
             try:
                 return datetime.strptime(dstr, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
             except ValueError:
                 return None
         
         def date_to_str(dateobj):
             return dateobj.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
         # Read and write functions for data files
         
         def read_books():
             books = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'books.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return books
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     fields = line.split('|')
                     if len(fields) != 10:
                         continue
                     books.append({
                         'book_id': int(fields[0]),
                         'title': fields[1],
                         'author': fields[2],
                         'isbn': fields[3],
                         'genre': fields[4],
                         'publisher': fields[5],
                         'year': int(fields[6]),
                         'description': fields[7],
                         'status': fields[8],
                         'avg_rating': float(fields[9])
                     })
             return books
         
         def write_books(books):
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'books.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for book in books:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(book['book_id']),
                         book['title'],
                         book['author'],
                         book['isbn'],
                         book['genre'],
                         book['publisher'],
                         str(book['year']),
                         book['description'],
                         book['status'],
                         f"{book['avg_rating']:.2f}"
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_users():
             users = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'users.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return users
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     fields = line.split('|')
                     if len(fields) != 4:
                         continue
                     users.append({
                         'username': fields[0],
                         'email': fields[1],
                         'phone': fields[2],
                         'address': fields[3]
                     })
             return users
         
         def write_users(users):
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'users.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for user in users:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         user['username'],
                         user['email'],
                         user['phone'],
                         user['address']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_borrowings():
             borrowings = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'borrowings.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return borrowings
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     fields = line.split('|')
                     if len(fields) != 8:
                         continue
                     borrowings.append({
                         'borrow_id': int(fields[0]),
                         'username': fields[1],
                         'book_id': int(fields[2]),
                         'borrow_date': fields[3],
                         'due_date': fields[4],
                         'return_date': fields[5],
                         'status': fields[6],
                         'fine_amount': float(fields[7])
                     })
             return borrowings
         
         def write_borrowings(borrowings):
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'borrowings.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for borrow in borrowings:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(borrow['borrow_id']),
                         borrow['username'],
                         str(borrow['book_id']),
                         borrow['borrow_date'],
                         borrow['due_date'],
                         borrow['return_date'],
                         borrow['status'],
                         f"{borrow['fine_amount']:.2f}"
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_reservations():
             reservations = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'reservations.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return reservations
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     fields = line.split('|')
                     if len(fields) != 5:
                         continue
                     reservations.append({
                         'reservation_id': int(fields[0]),
                         'username': fields[1],
                         'book_id': int(fields[2]),
                         'reservation_date': fields[3],
                         'status': fields[4]
                     })
             return reservations
         
         def write_reservations(reservations):
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'reservations.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for res in reservations:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(res['reservation_id']),
                         res['username'],
                         str(res['book_id']),
                         res['reservation_date'],
                         res['status']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_reviews():
             reviews = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'reviews.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return reviews
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     fields = line.split('|')
                     if len(fields) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         reviews.append({
                             'review_id': int(fields[0]),
                             'username': fields[1],
                             'book_id': int(fields[2]),
                             'rating': int(fields[3]),
                             'review_text': fields[4],
                             'review_date': fields[5]
                         })
                     except ValueError:
                         continue
             return reviews
         
         def write_reviews(reviews):
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'reviews.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for review in reviews:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(review['review_id']),
                         review['username'],
                         str(review['book_id']),
                         str(review['rating']),
                         review['review_text'],
                         review['review_date']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         def read_fines():
             fines = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'fines.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return fines
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line = line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     fields = line.split('|')
                     if len(fields) != 6:
                         continue
                     try:
                         fines.append({
                             'fine_id': int(fields[0]),
                             'username': fields[1],
                             'borrow_id': int(fields[2]),
                             'amount': float(fields[3]),
                             'status': fields[4],
                             'date_issued': fields[5]
                         })
                     except ValueError:
                         continue
             return fines
         
         def write_fines(fines):
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'fines.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for fine in fines:
                     line = '|'.join([
                         str(fine['fine_id']),
                         fine['username'],
                         str(fine['borrow_id']),
                         f"{fine['amount']:.2f}",
                         fine['status'],
                         fine['date_issued']
                     ])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         
         # Routes
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard_page():
             if 'username' not in session:
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=session['username'])
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def book_catalog_page():
             books = read_books()
             simple_books = [{
                 'book_id': b['book_id'],
                 'title': b['title'],
                 'author': b['author'],
                 'status': b['status']
             } for b in books]
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=simple_books)
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>')
         def book_details_page(book_id):
             books = read_books()
             book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)
             if book is None:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
             # Get reviews for this book
             reviews = read_reviews()
             book_reviews = [r for r in reviews if r['book_id'] == book_id]
             return render_template('book_details.html', book=book, reviews=book_reviews)
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def process_borrow_request(book_id):
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
             books = read_books()
             book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)
             if book is None or book['status'] != 'Available':
                 flash('Book not available for borrowing.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 # Show borrow confirmation page
                 due_date = datetime.now().date() + timedelta(days=14)
                 due_date_str = date_to_str(due_date)
                 return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book, due_date=due_date_str)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 current_user = session['username']
                 borrowings = read_borrowings()
                 # Ensure user does not have an active borrow for this book
                 active_borrow = next((b for b in borrowings if b['username'] == current_user and b['book_id'] == book_id and b['status'] == 'Active'), None)
                 if active_borrow:
                     flash('You already have an active borrow for this book.')
                     return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings_page'))
         
                 # Update book status
                 for b in books:
                     if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                         b['status'] = 'Borrowed'
                         break
                 write_books(books)
         
                 new_borrow_id = max([b['borrow_id'] for b in borrowings] or [0]) + 1
                 borrow_date = datetime.now().date()
                 due_date = borrow_date + timedelta(days=14)
                 new_borrow = {
                     'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,
                     'username': current_user,
                     'book_id': book_id,
                     'borrow_date': date_to_str(borrow_date),
                     'due_date': date_to_str(due_date),
                     'return_date': '',
                     'status': 'Active',
                     'fine_amount': 0.0
                 }
                 borrowings.append(new_borrow)
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
                 flash('Book borrowed successfully.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings_page'))
         
         @app.route('/my_borrows')
         def my_borrowings_page():
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
         
             borrow_context = []
             today = datetime.now().date()
         
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] != current_user:
                     continue
                 book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                 # Update status if overdue
                 if b['status'] == 'Active':
                     due_date_obj = str_to_date(b['due_date'])
                     if due_date_obj and today > due_date_obj:
                         b['status'] = 'Overdue'
                 borrow_context.append({
                     'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': book_title,
                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                     'due_date': b['due_date'],
                     'status': b['status'],
                     'fine_amount': b['fine_amount']
                 })
             return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrows=borrow_context)
         
         @app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def return_book(borrow_id):
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
             borrow = next((b for b in borrowings if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id and b['username'] == current_user), None)
             if borrow is None:
                 flash('Borrowing record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings_page'))
             if borrow['status'] not in ['Active', 'Overdue']:
                 flash('This borrow is not active or overdue.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings_page'))
         
             # Update borrow's return_date
             return_date = datetime.now().date()
             borrow['return_date'] = date_to_str(return_date)
             borrow['status'] = 'Returned'
         
             # Update book status to Available
             for b in books:
                 if b['book_id'] == borrow['book_id']:
                     b['status'] = 'Available'
                     break
         
             # Calculate fine if overdue
             due_date_obj = str_to_date(borrow['due_date'])
             days_overdue = 0
             if due_date_obj and return_date > due_date_obj:
                 days_overdue = (return_date - due_date_obj).days
             fine_amount = days_overdue * 1.0  # Assuming $1 per day overdue
             borrow['fine_amount'] = fine_amount
         
             write_borrowings(borrowings)
             write_books(books)
         
             # Create fine record if needed
             if fine_amount > 0:
                 fines = read_fines()
                 new_fine_id = max([f['fine_id'] for f in fines] or [0]) + 1
                 fines.append({
                     'fine_id': new_fine_id,
                     'username': current_user,
                     'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                     'amount': fine_amount,
                     'status': 'Unpaid',
                     'date_issued': date_to_str(return_date)
                 })
                 write_fines(fines)
                 flash(f'Book returned with a fine of ${fine_amount:.2f}.')
             else:
                 flash('Book returned successfully with no fines.')
         
             return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings_page'))
         
         @app.route('/my_reservations')
         def my_reservations_page():
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']

             reservation_context = []

         @app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])

             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             reservations = read_reservations()
             reservation = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id and r['username'] == current_user), None)

         @app.route('/my_reviews')
         def my_reviews_page():
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             reviews = read_reviews()
             books = read_books()
         
             reviews_context = []
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['username'] != current_user:
                     continue
                 book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == r['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                 reviews_context.append({
                     'review_id': r['review_id'],
                     'book_id': r['book_id'],
                     'book_title': book_title,
                     'rating': r['rating'],
                     'review_text': r['review_text']
                 })
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=reviews_context)
         
         @app.route('/write_review/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review_page(book_id):
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             books = read_books()
             book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
         
             reviews = read_reviews()
             existing_review = next((r for r in reviews if r['username'] == current_user and r['book_id'] == book_id), None)
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 try:
                     rating_raw = request.form.get('rating')
                     rating = int(rating_raw) if rating_raw and rating_raw.isdigit() and 1 <= int(rating_raw) <= 5 else 0
                 except ValueError:
                     rating = 0
                 review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
         
                 if rating == 0 or not review_text:
                     flash('Please provide a rating between 1 and 5 and a review text.')
                     return render_template('write_review.html', book=book, existing_review=existing_review)
         
                 today_str = date_to_str(datetime.now().date())
         
                 if existing_review:
                     # Update existing review
                     existing_review['rating'] = rating
                     existing_review['review_text'] = review_text
                     existing_review['review_date'] = today_str
                 else:
                     new_review_id = max([r['review_id'] for r in reviews] or [0]) + 1
                     new_review = {
                         'review_id': new_review_id,
                         'username': current_user,
                         'book_id': book_id,
                         'rating': rating,
                         'review_text': review_text,
                         'review_date': today_str
                     }
                     reviews.append(new_review)
         
                 write_reviews(reviews)
                 flash('Review submitted successfully.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_reviews_page'))
         
             # GET
             return render_template('write_review.html', book=book, existing_review=existing_review)
         
         @app.route('/delete_review/<int:review_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def delete_review(review_id):
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             reviews = read_reviews()
             review = next((r for r in reviews if r['review_id'] == review_id and r['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not review:
                 flash('Review not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_reviews_page'))
             reviews.remove(review)
             write_reviews(reviews)
             flash('Review deleted successfully.')
             return redirect(url_for('my_reviews_page'))
         
         @app.route('/profile')
         def user_profile_page():
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             users = read_users()
             user_profile = next((u for u in users if u['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not user_profile:
                 flash('User profile not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
             # Borrow history
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
             borrow_history_context = []
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] != current_user:
                     continue
                 if b['status'] != 'Returned':
                     continue
                 book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                 borrow_history_context.append({
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': book_title,
                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                     'return_date': b['return_date']
                 })
         
             return render_template('profile.html', user_profile=user_profile, borrow_history=borrow_history_context)
         
         @app.route('/profile/update', methods=['POST'])
         def update_profile():
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
         
             email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
             phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()
             address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()
         
             if not email or not phone or not address:
                 flash('Please fill all fields.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
             users = read_users()
             user = next((u for u in users if u['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not user:
                 flash('User not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
             user['email'] = email
             user['phone'] = phone
             user['address'] = address
             write_users(users)
             flash('Profile updated successfully.')
             return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def payment_confirmation_page(fine_id):
             if 'username' not in session:
                 flash('Please login first.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
             current_user = session['username']
             fines = read_fines()
             fine = next((f for f in fines if f['fine_id'] == fine_id and f['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not fine:
                 flash('Fine record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # Update fine status to Paid
                 fine['status'] = 'Paid'
                 write_fines(fines)
                 flash('Fine payment successful!')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
             # GET
             return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine=fine)
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         <!DOCTYPE html>
         <html lang="en">
         <head>
             <meta charset="UTF-8">
             <title>My Profile</title>
         </head>
         <body>
             <div id="profile-page">
                 <h1>My Profile</h1>
                 <div id="profile-username">Username: {{ user_profile.username }}</div>
                 <form method="POST" action="{{ url_for('update_profile') }}">
                     <label for="profile-email">Email:</label>
                     <input type="email" id="profile-email" name="email" value="{{ user_profile.email }}" required />
                     <br/>
                     <label for="profile-phone">Phone:</label>
                     <input type="text" id="profile-phone" name="phone" value="{{ user_profile.phone }}" required />
                     <br/>
                     <label for="profile-address">Address:</label>
                     <input type="text" id="profile-address" name="address" value="{{ user_profile.address }}" required />
                     <br/>
                     <button id="update-profile-button" type="submit">Update Profile</button>
                 </form>
                 <h2>Borrow History</h2>
                 <div id="borrow-history">
                     {% if borrow_history %}
                     <ul>
                         {% for borrow in borrow_history %}
                         <li>{{ borrow.title }}: Borrowed on {{ borrow.borrow_date }}, Returned on {{ borrow.return_date }}</li>
                         {% endfor %}
                     </ul>
                     {% else %}

         # Helper functions for file operations and data parsing
         
         def read_users():
             users = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'users.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return users
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     fields = line.split('|')
                     if len(fields) != 4:
                         continue
                     user = {
                         'username': fields[0],
                         'email': fields[1],
                         'phone': fields[2],
                         'address': fields[3]
                     }
                     users.append(user)
             return users
         
         def write_users(users):
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'users.txt')
             with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for u in users:
                     line = '|'.join([u['username'], u['email'], u['phone'], u['address']])
                     f.write(line + '\n')
         
         def read_books():
             books = []
             path = os.path.join(data_dir, 'books.txt')
             if not os.path.exists(path):
                 return books
             with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:

                     if not line:
                         continue

                     except ValueError:
                         continue
             return books

             return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
         # 2. dashboard_page - GET route with username context
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard_page():
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=current_user)
         
         # 3. book_catalog_page - GET route with books list
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def book_catalog_page():
             books = read_books()
             # Simplify data as per context: book_id, title, author, status
             simple_books = [{
                 'book_id': b['book_id'],
                 'title': b['title'],
                 'author': b['author'],
                 'status': b['status']
             } for b in books]
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=simple_books)
         
         # 4. book_details_page - GET /book/<int:book_id>
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>')
         def book_details_page(book_id):
             books = read_books()
             book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
         
             reviews = read_reviews()
             book_reviews = [r for r in reviews if r['book_id'] == book_id]
         
             # Compose reviews context dictionary with specified fields
             reviews_context = []
             for r in book_reviews:
                 reviews_context.append({
                     'review_id': r['review_id'],
                     'username': r['username'],
                     'rating': r['rating'],
                     'review_text': r['review_text'],
                     'review_date': r['review_date']
                 })
             return render_template('book_details.html', book=book, reviews=reviews_context)
         
         # 5. borrow_confirmation_page - GET /borrow/<int:book_id>
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET'])
         def borrow_confirmation_page(book_id):
             books = read_books()
             book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
             # Calculate due_date 14 days from today
             due_date = datetime.now().date() + timedelta(days=14)
             due_date_str = due_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             # Pass only book_id, title, author as context
             simple_book = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author']
             }
             return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=simple_book, due_date=due_date_str)
         
         # 6. process_borrow_request - POST /borrow/<int:book_id>
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def process_borrow_request(book_id):
             books = read_books()
             book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
         
             # Check if book is available
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 flash('Book is not available for borrow.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book_id))
         
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             # Generate new borrow_id
             new_borrow_id = max([b['borrow_id'] for b in borrowings], default=0) + 1
         
             borrow_date = datetime.now().date()
             due_date = borrow_date + timedelta(days=14)
         
             new_borrow = {
                 'borrow_id': new_borrow_id,
                 'username': current_user,
                 'book_id': book_id,
                 'borrow_date': date_to_str(borrow_date),
                 'due_date': date_to_str(due_date),
                 'return_date': '',
                 'status': 'Active',
                 'fine_amount': 0.0
             }
         
             borrowings.append(new_borrow)
             write_borrowings(borrowings)
         
             # Update book status to Borrowed
             for b in books:
                 if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                     b['status'] = 'Borrowed'
                     break
             write_books(books)
         
             simple_book = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author']
             }
             due_date_str = date_to_str(due_date)
             flash(f'Successfully borrowed {book["title"]}. Due date: {due_date_str}')
             return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=simple_book, due_date=due_date_str)
         
         # 7. my_borrowings_page - GET /my_borrows
         @app.route('/my_borrows')
         def my_borrowings_page():
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
         
             # Filter borrowings for current user
             user_borrows = [b for b in borrowings if b['username'] == current_user]
         
             # Update borrowing status to Overdue if due date < today and not returned
             today = datetime.now().date()
             updated = False
             for b in user_borrows:
                 if b['status'] == 'Active':
                     due_date = str_to_date(b['due_date'])
                     if due_date and due_date < today:
                         b['status'] = 'Overdue'
                         # fine calculation: $1 per day overdue
                         days_overdue = (today - due_date).days
                         fine_amount = float(days_overdue) * 1.0
                         b['fine_amount'] = fine_amount
                         updated = True
             if updated:
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
         
             # Compose context with required fields
             borrow_context = []
             for b in user_borrows:
                 book = next((bk for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), None)
                 title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'
                 borrow_context.append({
                     'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': title,
                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                     'due_date': b['due_date'],
                     'status': b['status'],
                     'fine_amount': b['fine_amount']
                 })
         
             return render_template('my_borrows.html', borrows=borrow_context)
         
         # 8. return_book - POST /return/<int:borrow_id>
         @app.route('/return/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def return_book(borrow_id):
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
             fines = read_fines()
         
             borrow = next((b for b in borrowings if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id and b['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not borrow:
                 flash('Borrow record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings_page'))
         
             if borrow['status'] == 'Returned':
                 flash('This book has already been returned.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_borrowings_page'))
         
             # Mark return date
             return_date = datetime.now().date()
             borrow['return_date'] = date_to_str(return_date)
         
             # Update status
             if borrow['status'] == 'Overdue':
                 # Must pay fine - create fine if not present
                 existing_fine = next((f for f in fines if f['borrow_id'] == borrow_id and f['username'] == current_user and f['status'] == 'Unpaid'), None)
                 if not existing_fine and borrow['fine_amount'] > 0:
                     # Create new fine
                     new_fine_id = max([f['fine_id'] for f in fines], default=0) + 1
                     fine_record = {
                         'fine_id': new_fine_id,
                         'username': current_user,
                         'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                         'amount': borrow['fine_amount'],
                         'status': 'Unpaid',
                         'date_issued': date_to_str(datetime.now().date())
                     }
                     fines.append(fine_record)
                     write_fines(fines)
                 # Status remains Overdue (not full returned because of fine unpaid)
             else:
                 borrow['status'] = 'Returned'
         
             write_borrowings(borrowings)
         
             # Update book status to Available
             for b in books:
                 if b['book_id'] == borrow['book_id']:
                     b['status'] = 'Available'
                     break
             write_books(books)
         
             borrow_context = {
                 'borrow_id': borrow['borrow_id'],
                 'book_id': borrow['book_id'],
                 'title': next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == borrow['book_id']), 'Unknown'),
                 'return_date': borrow['return_date'],
                 'status': borrow['status'],
                 'fine_amount': borrow['fine_amount']
             }
         
             flash('Book return processed. Thank you!')
             return render_template('return_confirmation.html', borrow=borrow_context)
         
         # 9. my_reservations_page - GET /my_reservations
         @app.route('/my_reservations')
         def my_reservations_page():
             reservations = read_reservations()
             books = read_books()
         
             user_reservs = [r for r in reservations if r['username'] == current_user]
         
             reservation_context = []
             for r in user_reservs:
                 book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), None)
                 title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'
                 reservation_context.append({
                     'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                     'book_id': r['book_id'],
                     'title': title,
                     'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],
                     'status': r['status']
                 })
         
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', reservations=reservation_context)
         
         # 10. cancel_reservation - POST /cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>
         @app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             reservations = read_reservations()
             res = next((r for r in reservations if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id and r['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not res:
                 flash('Reservation not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_reservations_page'))
         
             if res['status'] == 'Cancelled':
                 flash('Reservation already cancelled.')
                 return redirect(url_for('my_reservations_page'))
         
             res['status'] = 'Cancelled'
             write_reservations(reservations)
         
             flash('Reservation cancelled successfully.')
         
             # After cancellation, reload updated reservations list
             return my_reservations_page()
         
         # 11. my_reviews_page - GET /my_reviews
         @app.route('/my_reviews')
         def my_reviews_page():
             reviews = read_reviews()
             books = read_books()
         
             user_reviews = [r for r in reviews if r['username'] == current_user]
             reviews_context = []
             for r in user_reviews:
                 book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), None)
                 book_title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'
                 reviews_context.append({
                     'review_id': r['review_id'],
                     'book_title': book_title,
                     'rating': r['rating'],
                     'review_text': r['review_text']
                 })
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', reviews=reviews_context)
         
         # 12 & 13. write_review_page(GET), submit_review(POST) for /write_review/<int:book_id>
         @app.route('/write_review/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review_page(book_id):
             books = read_books()
             book = next((b for b in books if b['book_id'] == book_id), None)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_catalog_page'))
         
             # POST: process submitted review
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 rating_raw = request.form.get('rating')
                 review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
         
                 try:
                     rating = int(rating_raw)
                     if rating < 1 or rating > 5:
                         flash('Rating must be between 1 and 5.')
                         return render_template('write_review.html', book={ 'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']})
                 except:
                     flash('Invalid rating value.')
                     return render_template('write_review.html', book={ 'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']})
         
                 if not review_text:
                     flash('Review text cannot be empty.')
                     return render_template('write_review.html', book={ 'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']})
         
                 reviews = read_reviews()
         
                 # Check if user has already reviewed this book (exact specification does not clarify if editing or multiple allowed, assuming edit allowed)
                 existing_review = next((r for r in reviews if r['username'] == current_user and r['book_id'] == book_id), None)
         
                 today_str = datetime.now().date().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
                 if existing_review:
                     # Update existing review
                     existing_review['rating'] = rating
                     existing_review['review_text'] = review_text
                     existing_review['review_date'] = today_str
                 else:
                     # Add new review
                     new_review_id = max([r['review_id'] for r in reviews], default=0) + 1
                     new_review = {
                         'review_id': new_review_id,
                         'username': current_user,
                         'book_id': book_id,
                         'rating': rating,
                         'review_text': review_text,
                         'review_date': today_str
                     }
                     reviews.append(new_review)
         
                 write_reviews(reviews)
         
                 flash('Your review has been submitted.')
                 return redirect(url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book_id))
         
             # GET: display review form
             simple_book = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author']
             }
             return render_template('write_review.html', book=simple_book)
         
         # 14. user_profile_page - GET /profile
         @app.route('/profile')
         def user_profile_page():
             users = read_users()
             user_profile = next((u for u in users if u['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not user_profile:
                 flash('User profile not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
         
             user_borrow_history = [b for b in borrowings if b['username'] == current_user and b['status'] in ('Returned', 'Overdue')]
             borrow_history_context = []
             for b in user_borrow_history:
                 book = next((bk for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), None)
                 title = book['title'] if book else 'Unknown'
                 borrow_history_context.append({
                     'book_id': b['book_id'],
                     'title': title,
                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                     'return_date': b['return_date']
                 })
         
             return render_template('profile.html', user_profile=user_profile, borrow_history=borrow_history_context)
         
         # 15. update_profile - POST /profile/update
         @app.route('/profile/update', methods=['POST'])
         def update_profile():
             email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
             phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()
             address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()
         
             users = read_users()
             user_profile = next((u for u in users if u['username'] == current_user), None)
         
             if not user_profile:
                 flash('User profile not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
             # Validate basic email presence
             if not email:
                 flash('Email cannot be empty.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
             user_profile['email'] = email
             user_profile['phone'] = phone
             user_profile['address'] = address
         
             write_users(users)
         
             flash('Profile updated successfully.')
             return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
         # 16. payment_confirmation_page - GET /payment/<int:fine_id>
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['GET'])
         def payment_confirmation_page(fine_id):
             fines = read_fines()
             fine = next((f for f in fines if f['fine_id'] == fine_id and f['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not fine:
                 flash('Fine record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
             fine_context = {
                 'fine_id': fine['fine_id'],
                 'amount': fine['amount']
             }
         
             return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine=fine_context)
         
         # 17. confirm_payment - POST /payment/<int:fine_id>
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_payment(fine_id):
             fines = read_fines()
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
         
             fine = next((f for f in fines if f['fine_id'] == fine_id and f['username'] == current_user), None)
             if not fine:
                 flash('Fine record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
             if fine['status'] == 'Paid':
                 flash('This fine has already been paid.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
             # Mark fine as paid
             fine['status'] = 'Paid'
         
             # Also update borrowings status: if overdue and paid, mark as Returned
             borrow = next((b for b in borrowings if b['borrow_id'] == fine['borrow_id']), None)
             if borrow and borrow['status'] == 'Overdue':
                 borrow['status'] = 'Returned'
         
             write_fines(fines)
             write_borrowings(borrowings)
         
             flash('Fine payment successful. Thank you!')
             return redirect(url_for('user_profile_page'))
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
